  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0a0afd1d-13d9-416f-9e21-45450415718b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_685529969" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685529969" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685529969?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685529969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11700891952879162564"><br/><b>During this book I was either</b><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431736ra/866565.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <b>Or</b>
  <br/>
</p><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/642236.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Yes, it was a perfect mix of funny and sexy.</b><br/><br/>Which, in my opinion, is something that doesn't come around often while reading erotica. So that's already one of the main reasons why enjoyed reading this story so much.<br/><br/>♦ <b>If you're going to read this book, I would suggest that you not read it in a train full of people, or any other public place for that matter.</b> ♦<br/><br/>Unless, of course, you don't mind people casting funny looks at you when you suddenly burst ou</p></span>
  <span id="freeText11700891952879162564" style="display:none"><br><b>During this book I was either</b><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431736ra/866565.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>Or</b>
  <br>
</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/642236.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Yes, it was a perfect mix of funny and sexy.</b><br><br>Which, in my opinion, is something that doesn't come around often while reading erotica. So that's already one of the main reasons why enjoyed reading this story so much.<br><br>♦ <b>If you're going to read this book, I would suggest that you not read it in a train full of people, or any other public place for that matter.</b> ♦<br><br>Unless, of course, you don't mind people casting funny looks at you when you suddenly burst out laughing. <i>Then</i> I' suggest that you <i>do</i> read it in public.<br><br>Going in this story, I had no idea what to expect, but it turned out to be a fun, refreshing and highly entertaining ride! It was the perfect kind of feel good-story that we all sometimes need between reading some of those darker, more depressing reads. ;)<br><br>♦ <b>Lex Easton</b> is a New York fashion designer and a true Manhattanite. For years she's been buying the fabrics for her couture fashion line Easton Essentials from the Italian Giradoli Garment Company. Now, for some reason, the Girasoli Company has decided to cancel their business arrangement. But since they deliver the best materials and since New York Fashion Week is approaching, Lex is desperate to do whatever it takes in order to get her next shipment of fabrics. <br><br>♦ <b>Prince Massimo Tittoni</b> is a notorious playboy whose numerous adventures appear almost daily in the world wide press. He's filthy rich, a little arrogant and sexy as hell. He's also the CEO of Girasoli Garment Company and therefore the person Lex needs to convince in order to maintain their business arrangement. <br><br>So, in order to convince the Prince, Lex has decided to go over to Italy so she can meet the CEO in person... But will they she able to keep her business trip strictly professional? <br><br>♦<br><br>I loved the easy banter between Lex and Masi. They loved provocing each other and pushing each other's limits and it was fun witnessing which one of the two would snap first. Since the story is written in alternating point of views, we find out that both characters were obviously attracted to each other but that they each have their own reasons for keeping their distance at first. That's why their was a lot of back and forth going on between the two of them before they finally gave in to the attraction.<br><br>The sex scenes were hot, albeit them being a little over the top in a give-it-to-me-baby kind of way. Not that that ever bothered me. But there was one particular scene that had me going</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431736ra/866566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Balls. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That's the only thing I'm going to say about it, and if you've read the book, you'll know what I mean, LOL. <br><br>Other than that, I can honestly say that I really enjoyed this entertaining read. Based on the introductions of Lex's friends and fellow Manhanttanites, I'm already looking forward to reading their stories in the rest of the series!<br><br><br>There was <b>no cliffhanger</b>. In fact there was even a very sweet, perhaps maybe a little too cheesy (for my liking), <b>happy ending</b>.<br><br><br>As Lex would say,<br><br><i>"I came, I saw, I came again. I have things to do."</i><br><br>And now I'm off to read the next part of The Manhattanites!<br><br><br>xoxo. <br><br><br>♦ <b>CASTING:</b> ♦<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866567.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866568.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>3.5-4 STARS.</b><br><br><br><i>**Copy courtesy of the author via Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review**</i></p></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_696776928" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/696776928" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/696776928?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=arc-gifted">arc-gifted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=lol-funny">lol-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=sexy-suit-and-ties">sexy-suit-and-ties</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696776928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13252102706344053823"><b>~Copy provided by Author via Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review~<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395426i/761624._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>♥♥♥ 3.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445490450ra/16660516.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When I started this book, I didn't expect to laugh <b>so</b> much. This is an <b>erotica</b>, so of course there was some sex scenes (which were quite <b>hot!</b>). But it wasn't <b>overloaded</b> with sex, just a lot of talk about sex and <b>crude</b> language. But it was also very <b>funny</b>, well to me anyways.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433334i/871968._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To start with the story, <b>Lex Easton</b> is a fashion designer from New York. She is the owner of <b>Easton's Essentials</b> and has been buying her</span>
  <span id="freeText13252102706344053823" style="display:none"><b>~Copy provided by Author via Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review~<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395426i/761624._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♥♥♥ 3.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445490450ra/16660516.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I started this book, I didn't expect to laugh <b>so</b> much. This is an <b>erotica</b>, so of course there was some sex scenes (which were quite <b>hot!</b>). But it wasn't <b>overloaded</b> with sex, just a lot of talk about sex and <b>crude</b> language. But it was also very <b>funny</b>, well to me anyways.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433334i/871968._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To start with the story, <b>Lex Easton</b> is a fashion designer from New York. She is the owner of <b>Easton's Essentials</b> and has been buying her fabric from the Italian textile complany, <b>Girasoli</b>. Fashion week is fast approaching but she has yet to recieve her fabric order to create her samples for the line. When she calls to ask about her order, Prince Massimo Tuttoni, <b>(whom she has had a crush on and named her B.O.B after.)</b> responds the order will <b>not</b> be delivered... <b>ever</b>. Their business contract has been terminated. Outraged, Lex goes to Italy to confront him in person and to <b>demand</b> she get her fabric.<br><br>Lex was quite a <b>fiesty</b> character. She definitely wasn't <b>shy</b> when it came to getting what she wants. But when it came to <b>cameras</b> and the <b>spotlight</b>, she would rather run and hide. She had a difficult upbringing with both parents being <b>famous</b>. She felt as though she was put under a <b>microscope</b>. So she stays away from the media. I liked her, she <b>wasn't</b> a whiney woman who couldn't make up her mind. She <b>knows</b> what she wants and <b>goes</b> out to get it. But <b>sometimes</b> she could be a bit <b>stubborn</b> when things didn't go her way, which I didn't really like.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433334i/871969._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then there is the <b>one</b> and only... the <b>Italian hunk</b> with the <b>package</b> the size of an <b>"evian water bottle"</b>, <b>Prince Massimo Tittoni</b>. He is the CEO of Girasoli Garment Company. He is arrogant and intense, known to be a <b>playboy</b> and eternal <b>bachelor</b>. Massi is <b>what</b> he was <b>raised</b> to be. He doesn't want to fall in love again after he was left <b>devastated</b> in the past. He wants to start his <b>own</b> fashion line using their textiles, so he is no longer selling it. But soon, he learns he may need Lex's <b>expertise</b> to pull it off. So he decides to <b>propose</b> a business agreement to her.<br><br>I am <b>so</b> happy we got to see <b>both</b> of the characters <b>pov</b>. Because at first, I did <b>not</b> like him. But once you see the <b>reasons</b> why they were both <b>fighting</b> the attraction, it was really <b>funny</b> to see them <b>push</b> each other's boundaries. He was still a bit of a <b>jerk</b> at times, but also could be quite <b>endearing</b> in others. So eventually I did end up <b>liking</b> him. They just made a <b>great</b> duo.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445490450ra/16660517.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, now moving on the <b>sex</b>.... what can I say. There were some scenes that were plenty <b>hot</b>! But it was really <b>over-the-top</b>. I liked the <b>threesome</b> scene thrown in this book, but the only thing I <b>didn't</b> like was that the girl involved kept yelling <b>"darlings"</b> to her lovers. It kinda killed it for me and I couldn't help but <b>giggle</b>. There wasn't a buttload of sex in this book but the scenes that there were, were just too <b>porno-ish</b> to me. I mean honestly, they needed a freaking <b>mop</b> with all the <b>squirting</b> that was happening. I started to wonder if Lex didn't have some sort of <b>water hose</b> in there. And then there was a scene involving Massi's <b>balls</b>, all I could think was... <b>is that possible??</b> I don't know if I was the only one thinking this, but I got so damn <b>curious</b> I had to google it to find out *don't judge me*... and it <b>was</b>!! I was like <b>"Lordy!!!"</b> And to those who have read it and know what I mean, I <b>hope</b> you don't think I'm stupid lol! So yeah, some pretty <b>hot</b> scenes. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/606924.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The whole story was a <b>bit</b> on the <b>fast</b> side, as in, Lex and Massi both fall in love <b>quickly</b>. I think because of the pace of the book, I had <b>trouble</b> really <b>connecting</b> with both characters. But it was still <b>entertaining</b> seeing both characters <b>interact</b>. The ending was bit too <b>cheesy</b> than what I would have liked. We'll see how the <b>next</b> book in this series turns out. If you are looking for a <b>fun, light, sexy</b> read, this is it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Note:</b> This book may not be for everyone, due to the explicit subject matter.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13252102706344053823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1394856159" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1394856159" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1394856159?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25679349-undressed">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Those looking for a sweet, straightforward standalone romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1394856159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5555487153342429695">***I received a complimentary ARC of this book from the publisher, through Netgalley.com, in exchange for honest feedback.***<br/><br/>Although this book isn't the first in the series, it can easily be read as a standalone novel. This is the first book that I've read in this series, or by this author. I didn't feel like I was missing anything critical to the story, despite having not read the earlier books. I'm sure I would have had more background information about Lex's friends and family, but I don't f</span>
  <span id="freeText5555487153342429695" style="display:none">***I received a complimentary ARC of this book from the publisher, through Netgalley.com, in exchange for honest feedback.***<br /><br />Although this book isn't the first in the series, it can easily be read as a standalone novel. This is the first book that I've read in this series, or by this author. I didn't feel like I was missing anything critical to the story, despite having not read the earlier books. I'm sure I would have had more background information about Lex's friends and family, but I don't feel like reading this book out of sequence took anything away from my enjoyment of this book.<br /><br />The heroine, Lex, has worked incredibly hard to reinvent herself after her famous rockstar father died, leaving Lex and her mother bankrupt, with only an inheritance of bad debt. After sinking what remains of her personal savings into rehabilitation centers to sober her mother up, she sets out to make something of herself. Through her sweat and tears, along with some financial help from a close friend, Lex is able to build her clothing line from the ground up. <br /><br />After a few years, Lex's company, Easton Essentials, is a mainstay in her corner of the fashion market. When her fabric supplier fails to deliver her order before thie season's big debut show, she knows that all of her hard work would be destroyed if she doesn't get that order filled. With the timeline growing ever nearer, she decides to fly to Italy to confront the arrogant business owner herself.<br /><br />Massimo is immediately taken aback by this brazen American beauty who's interrupted his vacation to demand that he fulfill her fabric order. He'd cancelled the order after Ms. Easton's company failed to pay for the order. While he feels sorry for this stunning woman, he cannot let his attraction to her cloud his judgment. He had plans to discontinue their business relationship in the near future anyway, as he had made the decision to take his business in a new direction. If everything went according to plans, he'd be marketing his own clothing line to compete with Easton Essentials.<br /><br />As I'm sure you can imagine, Lex and Massimo got off to a rocky start. From the beginning, their relationship was full of sexual tension and witty banter. These two loved to hate each other. There was never a dull moment as they verbally warred with each other and constantly tried to gain the upper hand.<br /><br />When they finally succumb to their passions, it was long over-due and scorching hot. However, the blissful new beginning doesn't last for long. Immediately the couple is thrown into a scandal of epic proportions. Lex is forced to leave Massimo while she attempts to do damage control and salvage her hard-earned reputation.<br /><br />For the most part, this story was a humorous, entertaining and sexy read. It was well-written and flowed well from one part to the next. I liked the characters and the storyline, but I never fell in love with them. It was a nice, sweet story, and a good choice for those days when you need to recover from a book hangover. It was straightforward and easy to read. Overall it was "good".<br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5555487153342429695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4322889282274530365" style="display:none"><b>4 Red Carpet Stars</b>	<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434131i/874111.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lex is the only daughter of an old music legend who killed himself a few years ago and left her and her mother without anything. <br>And being a Manhattan Socialite and with appearances to maintain, when she found herself with nothing she created a clothesline from nothing that is now starting to rise into stardom. But she is persistence and will fight for her dream… even if she has to go to Italy and try to convince the CEO herself. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434131i/874112.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The CEO is no one less than Prince Massimo, the ultimate billionaire hot playboy that even belongs to the Italian royalty. <br>And Massimo didn’t expect the CEO of Easton to be so stubborn… in fact, he didn’t even expected it would be a woman, and a hot one!!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434131ra/874113.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both of them are slightly troubled by past and unable to commit… but when feelings starts to get messed up, things start to heat and well… you can say that their professional relationship will never be the same. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/591886.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was way better than I was expecting it to be. (My expectations weren’t very high, I confess.)<br>There were basically two drastic speeds in this book: Extremely Hot and Extremely Funny. <br>It was a very entertaining reading with good steam in the middle. <br>I particularly liked the little explanation of the characters and the surroundings in the beginning of the book; it was a good change of pace. <br> <br>If you’re looking for a light, fun reading, this is without a doubt the book for you! ;) </span>

Prince Massimo Tutton owns the brand best Italian fabric.<br /><b>Secondary characters: </b> We have here a lot of good characters who have their stories in separate books.<br /><b>Steamy:</b> Hot and intense sexual scenes. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ We have here a lot of sexual scenes, all kinds, and threesome in which the main characters did not participate but are described from the outside. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Sensitive topic: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Love triangle:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Cheating:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Cliffhanger: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>HEA:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>For who I would recommend?</b> If you want to read some funny erotica with Italian style. <br /><br />***<br /><br /><b>About the plot:</b> When Lex Easton realizes that ordered by her fabrics will not arrive in time for Fashion Week, on which depends the future of her brand. She decides fly to Italy to directly convince an Italian prince, who is the owner.<br /><br />Despite her stubborn nature and biting tongue, Lex fails to do much beyond irritate the prince. Even worse she finds out that they want to create their brand and be her competition. <br /><br />Prince Massimo soft-heart, or perhaps his hard cock to American girl gives her a chance to prove herself. He takes her to manufacturing where he realizes that it is Lex who is the key to success. And that their attraction is mutual. Since that time, many things happen that are completely hot and crazy. <br /><br /><b>Final thoughts:</b> The biggest plus of this book is that it is fun. Internal deliberations of the heroine are priceless!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Earth to my muffin. Earth to my muffin! Do you remember this? I sure as hell don’t.”</i>
</b><br /><br />The second thing is that Italian hero is sooo sweet. His all Italian words inclusions just make me melts.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“In all honesty, about last night—you are easy to sleep next to. My bella smells fruity, and your skin is soft.””</i>
</b><br /><br />And it is kinky. As soon as you feel like you can count on it here. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Such a tight, hot mouth. My cock on your lips and down your throat will do you some good, bella. Your tongue is too sharp.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I really enjoyed their all interactions. Until the third part introduces the crazy plot and "almost" normal story starting of get ridiculous show. But probably in the style of Manhattan. It was fast, cliche and a little highly unlikely, but well, who cares... <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I professed love first, my principessa. But sì, tonight I will fuck you”</i>
</b><br /><br />So how to judge a book that sometimes has a ridiculous plot, but it is very funny? I circled between 3 and 4 stars. But I decided to rating to the benefit of the book. I felt that I had so much fun reading this, and when I was looking for something similar surely reach this author again.<br /><br /><b>Next in the series?</b> Yes. This series has more parts! Next M/M Romance Unsaid.<br /><br /><i>*ARC provided by Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.*</i></span>

  <span id="freeText6406783775465140667" style="display:none"><b>NOW THAT WAS A SCORCHER!!!!</b><br /><br />Story Rating 4.5 Stars<br />Character Rating 4.5 Stars<br />Romance Rating 5 Stars<br />Heat Level 5 Stars<br />Overall Rating 5 Stars<br /><br />This story was interesting the whole way through, not one boring spot in the whole book, I blew right through it. He was also very well built, wasn’t lacking in the male appendage department…he was huge…and he knew how to use it. *sigh*<br /><br />The heat level was <b>OVER THE TOP HOT!!</b> There was m/w/m scene that Lex watched from a hiding place that just about over heated my Kindle. WOW! The love scenes with Lex and Massimo were really hot and so well done that even my panties got wet…did I just say that? I love my erotica, and the author did not disappoint. <br /><br />Towards the end of the book, Lex and Massimo parted ways. I found myself shedding a tear or two, it really got to me. I was not certain what was going to happen between these two lovers, and then to my surprise the romance kicked in high gear and I was left with an ear to ear smile on my face. <br /><br />The ending was conclusive, nicely done and it left me feeling good, but I still wished that there would have been an epilogue, I just love reading about how happy the couples are and what is going on with them a few years down the road. Oh well, maybe next time. <br /><br />Looks as if I found myself another <b>FANTASTIC</b> must read author! Avery Aster did a splendid job on this book and I can hardly believe that this is her debut novel. She has found her niche and I look forward to reading many more of her <b>SCORCHING HOT</b> romances. <br /><br /><i>**A copy of this book was kindly provided by Avery Aster in exchange for and honest review**</i><br /><br /><br /></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer551685162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7603155046374277936"><b> 3.75 Stars</b> <br/><br/>I found Undressed to be a very sexy and saucy look into the world of fashion. The heroine, Lex can be a bitch when she needs to be and I was worried for a bit that she was never going to soften, but she did. Massimo, our hero is a prince and fabric exporter. He's known for being a playboy, but he's greatly misunderstood. I found him to be romantic to the bone. Chivalrous and dignified, qualities that sometimes caused him to take the wrong action when it came to love.<br/><br/>The sexual tensio</span>
  <span id="freeText7603155046374277936" style="display:none"><b> 3.75 Stars</b> <br /><br />I found Undressed to be a very sexy and saucy look into the world of fashion. The heroine, Lex can be a bitch when she needs to be and I was worried for a bit that she was never going to soften, but she did. Massimo, our hero is a prince and fabric exporter. He's known for being a playboy, but he's greatly misunderstood. I found him to be romantic to the bone. Chivalrous and dignified, qualities that sometimes caused him to take the wrong action when it came to love.<br /><br />The sexual tension is palpable and the passion is clear, but the cultural miscommunications lead to a debacle, the couple may not be able to fix.<br /><br />What I loved about Undressed:<br /><br />-Massimo sleeps with three Cane Corsos (big ass dogs) in his bed. <br />-Lex built her fashion label from nothing, helping her mother along the way.<br />-Lex is determined to be successful at any cost, which leads her to fly to Milan to deal with Massimo face to face. <br />-The author knows her shit about the fashion world, from fabrics to designers.<br />-Jemma. Massimo's employee and friend who helps Lex with all things Milanese. She's a great character.<br />-There's some very hot sex that includes a main character as a voyeur. I get to add the shelf "female ejaculation". Woohoo!<br />-I enjoyed the plot and the characters were very colorful.<br />-The author made some unpredictable choices that surprised me in a good way. <br /><br />What I didn't like about Undressed:<br /><br />-I would have liked to see Massimo's temper a bit more. He was always very calm.<br />-Where was all of Lex's fire when she should have been mad at Massimo?<br />-There was something strange during one of the sex scenes that I just can't fathom. It took me out of the book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When the couple is having sex, he inserts his "gigantic dick" AND BALLS into her "tight pussy". I don't have balls, but that sounds like it would hurt. And I've read a lot of erotica, <i>a lot</i>. And I've never read balls inserted for penetration. As a nurse, I'm perplexed.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />-Some of the dirty talk, I found strange. Both the Italian and the New Yorker said, "Come on" and "Let's Go" quite often. That's ball game chatter, not dirty talk.<br /><br /><br />I look forward to book 2.</span>

  <span id="freeText67495965725834480" style="display:none">Loved, loved, loved!! OMG am I kicking myself for waiting to read this because I thought it was a cliffy!!         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17379259-undressed">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer573527177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14636747782483533128">First off, I will say that this book was a real surprise for me. This was marketed as erotic romance, and while it is indeed graphic -- with a token menage a trois thrown in for good measure -- there are actually fewer sex scenes in this book compared to your standard erotic novel. <br/><br/>The second thing that was a surprise to me was the humor. It's brash, in-your-face and yes, often crude brand of humor, which not everyone might appreciate. If you're the type to get offended by this type of humor, th</span>
  <span id="freeText14636747782483533128" style="display:none">First off, I will say that this book was a real surprise for me. This was marketed as erotic romance, and while it is indeed graphic -- with a token menage a trois thrown in for good measure -- there are actually fewer sex scenes in this book compared to your standard erotic novel. <br /><br />The second thing that was a surprise to me was the humor. It's brash, in-your-face and yes, often crude brand of humor, which not everyone might appreciate. If you're the type to get offended by this type of humor, then this book might not be for you. <br /><br />That said, I really enjoyed this book. It has a lot of laugh-out-loud and "Oh no, she-did-not-just-say-that," moments throughout the book. The banter between the main characters, Lex, a fashion designer and Masi, a prince and CEO of a large Italian textile company, are fun to read and their romance was actually very sweet. Both are well developed and I was happy that the author did provide us with a believable back story of Lex and Masi. The ending was a bit cheesy for my taste but I think it worked out well. <br /><br />I will say that this book is not for everybody. If you're looking for something dark and has a lot of angst, this book isn't for you. This book is escapism in its purest form. So if you're looking to slip into another world where it's full glitz and full of fashionable and beautiful people, then you would really enjoy this book. I know, I did. <br /><br /><b>*This ARC was provided by Avery Aster through Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review.</b></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8689646428758605106">3.5 Stars.<br/><br/>Holy Sh!t, brace yourself people, this book takes erotica to a whole new level of lewd, crude and totally over the top, giggle until you wanna pee your pants smut. <br/><br/>Avery Aster certainly has imagination and boy is it vivid, and I literally lost count of the amount of WTF moments there are in this story. <br/><br/>Lex certainly isn't scared to speak her mind, and I found Massimo's internal dialogue at times LOL funny.   <span id="freeText8689646428758605106" style="display:none">3.5 Stars.<br /><br />Holy Sh!t, brace yourself people, this book takes erotica to a whole new level of lewd, crude and totally over the top, giggle until you wanna pee your pants smut. <br /><br />Avery Aster certainly has imagination and boy is it vivid, and I literally lost count of the amount of WTF moments there are in this story. <br /><br />Lex certainly isn't scared to speak her mind, and I found Massimo's internal dialogue at times LOL funny. I read the better part of this book curled up in my local coffee shop, and I cannot tell you how many funny looks I got sitting there giggling away to myself.<br /><br />This is an enjoyable XXX rated romp through the Italian and American fashion world, where everything is taken too the extreme, thoughts, feelings, orgasms and general sexual acrobatics, I read things in this book I didn't even realise were physically possible!!! one word "balls", you will know what I mean when you read the book ;-) <br /><br />If you are looking for a serious erotica book, this is not for you, but if you have an open mind, are looking for a few shocks, laughs and totally OTT characters then The Manhattanites Series will definitely be right up your street.<br /><br />Although this is mainly m/f erotica, there is a little menage action with some secondary characters. <br /><br />ARC provided by the author for an honest review.<br /><br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1357583061?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/31452668-samantha">Samantha</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1357583061" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10427380614593382582">If I recall correctly this is my first time reading anything by Avery Aster. While I liked her choice of a hero, Massimo is a great Italian man, I wasn't sold on her choice of heroine. The reason this book gets 3.5 soft and bored stars is because I just could not connect with Lex (Alexandra) no matter how hard I tried. Since she's from my area it shouldn't have been hard but she was just too much bull shit and that's coming from a ridiculously blunt and in-your-face extrovert bred in the NYC are</span>
  <span id="freeText10427380614593382582" style="display:none">If I recall correctly this is my first time reading anything by Avery Aster. While I liked her choice of a hero, Massimo is a great Italian man, I wasn't sold on her choice of heroine. The reason this book gets 3.5 soft and bored stars is because I just could not connect with Lex (Alexandra) no matter how hard I tried. Since she's from my area it shouldn't have been hard but she was just too much bull shit and that's coming from a ridiculously blunt and in-your-face extrovert bred in the NYC area. <br /><br />I wanted to love this book but Lex just got on my nerves more times than I could count and I did have a few issues with Massimo. I also had a few issues with the way the story was structured and it felt a bit amateur to me which caused more problems with my enjoyment. There's a happy ending, there's lots of sexual content, but this story just didn't work for me. <br /><br />I did like the movement between New York, Milan, and so forth as well as a little look in to the fashion world. I like the way Aster attempted to paint the characters in three dimensions rather than one. I also just liked the fact that Massimo continuously weaved Italian into his talking language because I do love Italian. Overall, I wasn't really sold on the story and didn't <b> feel</b> like I have with other stories such as Opening Up by Lauren Dane. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10712986180598355285">3.75 HEARTS<br/><br/>I’m all over the shop with my review for this book. It made me laugh out loud. It placed a smile on my face which stayed there for a damn long time.<br/><br/>However...<br/><br/>It did have its drawbacks. <br/><br/>There were so many pages that I loved in this book, but the sex unfortunately pulled me out of my enjoyment. He spoke with the most delicious accent and I loved how his dialogue was sprinkled with se</span>
  <span id="freeText10712986180598355285" style="display:none">3.75 HEARTS<br /><br />I’m all over the shop with my review for this book. It made me laugh out loud. It placed a smile on my face which stayed there for a damn long time.<br /><br />However...<br /><br />It did have its drawbacks. <br /><br />There were so many pages that I loved in this book, but the sex unfortunately pulled me out of my enjoyment. I hope I can do my best to explain my point of view. <br /><br />Italian Prince Massimo Tittoni was hot. SUPER HAWT. He spoke with the most delicious accent and I loved how his dialogue was sprinkled with sexy Italian words. And Lex? She was funny as hell. Not just a little bit funny, but HUGELY funny. <br /><br />The emotion between them is palpable, clearly written and believable. I swooned in anticipation for their happily ever after. But I found that things didn’t always add up and the sexual relationship between them wasn’t strong enough in the end.<br /><br />Now this book is naughty. It isn’t written with flowery words. It is all about tits and d*ck. And the sexual scenes are explicit. Yet the acts between Massimo and Lex are very few and far between. At times it felt like there was more sex between the side characters.I wanted more! For such an explicit book there wasn't enough sex between the protagonists.<br /><br />Massimo is also explained as being hung like an Evian bottle. And Lex hasn’t had sex in a while. So add those together and I anticipated a slow, sensual – yet explicit scene for their first time. <br /><br />I was wrong...and left with the impression that Lex’s vagina resemble a chasm of doom with everything she fit in there. I’ve never read a scene where a guy shoves his monster truck sized penis into a woman AS WELL as the berries. That was an eye opener. And although the scene was described as "making love" it just felt like sex to me.<br /><br />There were other bits and pieces I didn’t enjoy sexually speaking but I’m not going to go into detail because they are my own sexual preferences. And no, I’m not talking about the guy on guy scene – I loved that.<br /><br />BUT – apart from my aversion to the sex I did enjoy this book. <br /><br />I think Avery is a master of sarcastic humor. I loved her one-liners, Massimo, Lex, the writing style, the pace. The majority of the story was really great in my opinion and I am looking forward to the next in this series.<br /><br />Hotness Rating: <br />This is actually a hard one to rate. Its explicit nature deserves a 5, but there just wasn't enough actual sex to rate it that high. So maybe 4 *shrugs*</span>

<div id="review_553129329" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/553129329" />
    <a title="Jen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5962787-jen"><img alt="Jen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563496869p2/5962787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/553129329?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17379259-undressed">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=a-little-smutty">a-little-smutty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=arc-edelweiss">arc-edelweiss</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553129329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13807475500116857299"><b>3.5 Entertaining Stars</b><br/><br/><i>Undressed</i> is an extremely fast paced and sexy read, though I don’t think it’s everyone’s cuppa tea. Those who don’t find the fashion industry, well endowed Italian princes proven to induce “squirting” or an over the top happily ever after should probably steer clear.<br/><br/>Let’s start with Lex. She’s by far my favorite character and I loved her and her snarky group of friends. She’s made a name for herself in the fashion world, in spite of a difficult upbringing in the public eye,</span>
  <span id="freeText13807475500116857299" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Entertaining Stars</b><br /><br /><i>Undressed</i> is an extremely fast paced and sexy read, though I don’t think it’s everyone’s cuppa tea. Those who don’t find the fashion industry, well endowed Italian princes proven to induce “squirting” or an over the top happily ever after should probably steer clear.<br /><br />Let’s start with Lex. She’s by far my favorite character and I loved her and her snarky group of friends. She’s made a name for herself in the fashion world, in spite of a difficult upbringing in the public eye, via her talent and straight up working her ass off. No hand outs for this girl. When something gets in the way of her professional dreams she confronts it head on, which is exactly how she meets Italian playboy and BOB namesake Massimo Tittoni. In addition to being a hot and wealthy tabloid fixture, Massimo also owns the textile company and the fabric Lex needs to make her designs a success. When, deadline looming, Lex’s fabric is MIA she heads to Massimo’s private island off the coast of Italy to rectify the situation. Some people have it so rough!<br /><br />Lex is hot, Massimo’s hot and it’s an Ellora’s Cave novel. It’s not difficult to see where the story’s headed. In spite of that, sexy times between these two took a bit longer to get to than I’d expected, in a good way. Lex and Massimo run through every conceivable emotion as far as the other’s concerned, from anger to distrust to lust to hurt to love. And back again. <br /><br />I’m not exaggerating when I say this is a fast paced book. Lex and Massimo fall <b>IN LOVE</b> over the course of one week. During that week we’re also gifted with a threesome witnessed by Lex, Milan nightlife, two devious skanks looking to make a quick buck, a tabloid scandal involving a previously under the radar Lex and family drama. Oh, lots of fashion action takes place as well. There’s a lot packed into this story and that’s probably my biggest complaint. As entertaining as it was, I felt the connection between Lex and Massimo suffered because of it and I didn’t entirely buy the big finale HEA. <br /><br />In spite of some story issues I highly enjoyed <i>Undressed</i>. I’m already looking forward to reading about Lex’s friends (maybe?) as the series progresses. <br /><br /><i>This book provided from the Author and Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review.</i> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13807475500116857299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/545782145?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Janey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Janey" href="/user/show/15078846-janey">Janey</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer545782145" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2226825987782867247">Being keen to read “Undressed”, I was delighted to receive an ARC from the author for an honest review.<br/><br/>This was a very funny read..from the offset.. “Massimo, answer the flippin’ phone—you royal pain in my ass!” Lex Easton, owner of Easton Essentials and an Upper East Side designer, contacts Prince Massimo Tittoni directly to understand why his company had not fulfilled her fabric order to complete her new fashion brand. She is desperate to complete her samples for her up and coming fashion coll</span>
  <span id="freeText2226825987782867247" style="display:none">Being keen to read “Undressed”, I was delighted to receive an ARC from the author for an honest review.<br /><br />This was a very funny read..from the offset.. “Massimo, answer the flippin’ phone—you royal pain in my ass!” Lex Easton, owner of Easton Essentials and an Upper East Side designer, contacts Prince Massimo Tittoni directly to understand why his company had not fulfilled her fabric order to complete her new fashion brand. She is desperate to complete her samples for her up and coming fashion collection, showcasing in a few weeks. Following a misunderstanding during the initial phone conversation, Lex decided to travel to Massimo’s Isola di Girasoli, where he was on vacation.<br /><br />The dialogue was hysterical, including the constant internal musings. Lex had previously adoringly named her BOB “Masi’s salami”, which was confirmed on sight when she sneakily admired his “Evian bottle” on entering the garden pool at his “palace”!<br /><br />We are taken through their dancing interactions, with Italian subtext, fashionista name dropping and, above all, great humour. Needless to say the chemistry was off the scale..just how I like it! Be aware that our gorgeous Masi favours the “see you next Tuesday” word, and being British, I have to say consider yourself warned!<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed Avery’s writing style, and the fashion background just increased my interest. Her old &amp; new friends were intriguing characters, and I look forward to seeing how they may develop/feature in the upcoming series. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13115500697639012413">Okay, so it's a little confusing for me to start a series and read them out of order, but it worked, lol. I'm still a little confused about how to rate this book, but having said that, I think I liked this book more than the first. <br/><br/>Lex is struggling to keep her fashion company together. She's been working her ass off to keep it off the ground and has high hopes that with this next Fashion Week everything will pay off. However, her fabric provider has decided last minute he won't be sending her t</span>
  <span id="freeText13115500697639012413" style="display:none">Okay, so it's a little confusing for me to start a series and read them out of order, but it worked, lol. I'm still a little confused about how to rate this book, but having said that, I think I liked this book more than the first. <br /><br />Lex is struggling to keep her fashion company together. She's been working her ass off to keep it off the ground and has high hopes that with this next Fashion Week everything will pay off. However, her fabric provider has decided last minute he won't be sending her the fabrics. With no other choice, Lex leaves home and heads to Prince Massimo's to try to convince him to send the shipment. Little did she know this business adventure would be life altering, not only for her company but personally as well. <br /><br />I loved Prince Massimo. He was hot hot hot!! And Lex was strong willed and brave. I got a little confused because some of the things Lex did after her and Massimo got together didn't exactly seem like her, and some of the things Massimo said and did, didn't really seem like a Prince would do. I like them together, just some things that happened felt a little odd for the characters. <br /><br />I don't want to seem like I'm picking the story apart, it's just some things I noticed, but it was still a good story and I must say I liked it more than the second in the series. :) I think Blake's story should be interesting and can't wait to read it soon! :)</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ratherread" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ratherread" href="/user/show/7358237-ratherread">ratherread</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9254276158494600361">4.5 Stars! (I always round up)<br/><br/>I really liked this book. The story was great and I loved the characters. All the main characters are very lovable and good-hearted....and kinky, sexy, damaged and fun. This is a lite read with humor, sexual tension, erotica and a little angst. And my favorites: NO CLIFFHANGER AND A GREAT HEA!!! A nice break from some of the more emotionally intense stories that leave readers hanging, that are popular today. <br/><br/>I adore Lex and her 3 best friends. They have weathered a </span>
  <span id="freeText9254276158494600361" style="display:none">4.5 Stars! (I always round up)<br /><br />I really liked this book. The story was great and I loved the characters. All the main characters are very lovable and good-hearted....and kinky, sexy, damaged and fun. This is a lite read with humor, sexual tension, erotica and a little angst. And my favorites: NO CLIFFHANGER AND A GREAT HEA!!! A nice break from some of the more emotionally intense stories that leave readers hanging, that are popular today. <br /><br />I adore Lex and her 3 best friends. They have weathered a lot of life's storms together and stuck together to help each other. Each book in the series focuses on one of them. <br /><br />In "Undressed", Lex is a brilliant fashion designer, jaded by her wild rock star parent's self-destructive ways. Massimo is the wealthy prince of a small Italian island and owner of the world's finest textile company. He is also jaded by his father's philandering. <br /><br />They meet, fight, negotiate and after a lot of sexual tension, finally give into their attraction to each other and fall in love. But a scandal threatens to tear them apart, as well as destroy their business empires. <br /><br />This story has a great plot with lots of hot erotic fantasies. Now on to book 2 "Unscrupulous", Taddy's story.<br /><br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qsplug4wEVt6+0P7YYyuVNCPN6hYOC/2LDPsCXx34vLdO3ntdrm/MA4OLAnPPM5r+nllIXY4OZSZOm/lwvIyHg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TWPuSHiWxnvDurMKDrg8gtDLPNr+iEg/WDHIVE1Hv1o6kvIfAB9oELdP3PigCFy9+j1uU9CIXl3tOEu488Jvtg==')})
  }
